Sentence #41 (45 tokens):
1993 federal law
Monday's ruling was based on a 1993 federal law, the Religious Freedom Restoration Act, which prohibits federal actions that "substantially burden the exercise of religion" unless those actions are necessary to serve some compelling public interest.
